DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Set base directory
  ENV BASE_DIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      git \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-dev \
      build-essential \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install micromamba
  RUN wget -qO- https://micromamba.snakepit.net/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj bin/micromamba && \
      ./bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p ~/micromamba && \
      rm -f bin/micromamba
  # Clone repository with submodules
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git && \
      cd Baleen-FAST24 && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Set up environment
  COPY environment.yml $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && \
      micromamba env create -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      pip install jupyter
  # Download trace files
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/data
  RUN chmod +x get-tectonic.sh && \
      ./get-tectonic.sh && \
      chmod +x clean.sh
  # Setup reproduce script and make executable
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/notebooks/reproduce
  RUN chmod +x reproduce_commands.sh
  # Create getting-started script
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen/Baleen-FAST24\n\
  ./BCacheSim/run_py.sh py -B -m BCacheSim.cachesim.simulate_ap --config runs/example/rejectx/config.json' > getting-started.sh && \
      chmod +x getting-started.sh
  # Set default command
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", ". ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && /bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 1 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Set base directory
  ENV BASE_DIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      git \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-dev \
      build-essential \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install micromamba
  RUN wget -qO- https://micromamba.snakepit.net/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj bin/micromamba && \
      ./bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p ~/micromamba && \
      rm -f bin/micromamba
  # Clone repository with submodules
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git && \
      cd Baleen-FAST24 && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Set up environment
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && \
      micromamba env create -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      pip install jupyter
  # Download trace files
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/data
  RUN chmod +x get-tectonic.sh && \
      ./get-tectonic.sh && \
      chmod +x clean.sh
  # Setup reproduce script and make executable
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/notebooks/reproduce
  RUN chmod +x reproduce_commands.sh
  # Create getting-started script
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen/Baleen-FAST24\n\
  ./BCacheSim/run_py.sh py -B -m BCacheSim.cachesim.simulate_ap --config runs/example/rejectx/config.json' > getting-started.sh && \
      chmod +x getting-started.sh
  # Set default command
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", ". ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && /bin/bash"]

  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Set base directory
  ENV BASE_DIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      git \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.9 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-dev \
      build-essential \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install micromamba
  RUN wget -qO- https://micromamba.snakepit.net/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj bin/micromamba && \
      ./bin/micromamba shell init -s bash -p ~/micromamba && \
      rm -f bin/micromamba
  # Clone repository with submodules
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git && \
      cd Baleen-FAST24 && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Set up environment
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && \
      micromamba env create -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      pip install jupyter
  # Download trace files
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/data
  RUN chmod +x get-tectonic.sh && \
      ./get-tectonic.sh && \
      chmod +x clean.sh
  # Setup reproduce script and make executable
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/notebooks/reproduce
  RUN chmod +x reproduce_commands.sh
  # Create getting-started script
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen/Baleen-FAST24\n\
  ./BCacheSim/run_py.sh py -B -m BCacheSim.cachesim.simulate_ap --config runs/example/rejectx/config.json' > getting-started.sh && \
      chmod +x getting-started.sh
  # Set default command
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", ". ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && /bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Set base directory
  ENV BASE_DIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      git \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.9 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-dev \
      build-essential \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install micromamba with proper permissions and cleanup
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba && \
      wget -qO- https://micromamba.snakepit.net/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest | tar -xvj -C /opt/micromamba --strip-components=1 bin/micromamba && \
      /opt/micromamba/micromamba shell init -s bash -p ~/micromamba && \
      rm -rf /opt/micromamba
  # Clone repository with submodules
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git && \
      cd Baleen-FAST24 && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Set up environment
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && \
      micromamba env create -f BCacheSim/install/env_cachelib-py-3.11.yaml && \
      micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && \
      pip install jupyter
  # Download trace files
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/data
  RUN chmod +x get-tectonic.sh && \
      ./get-tectonic.sh && \
      chmod +x clean.sh
  # Setup reproduce script and make executable
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/notebooks/reproduce
  RUN chmod +x reproduce_commands.sh
  # Create getting-started script
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  . ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh\n\
  micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11\n\
  cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen/Baleen-FAST24\n\
  ./BCacheSim/run_py.sh py -B -m BCacheSim.cachesim.simulate_ap --config runs/example/rejectx/config.json' > getting-started.sh && \
      chmod +x getting-started.sh
  # Set default command
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", ". ~/micromamba/etc/profile.d/micromamba.sh && micromamba activate cachelib-py-3.11 && /bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Set base directory
  ENV BASE_DIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      git \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.9 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-dev \
      build-essential \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install micromamba with proper permissions and verification
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba && \
      chmod 755 /opt/micromamba && \
      wget -qO /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 https://micromamba.snakepit.net/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest && \
      (tar -xjf /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 -C /opt/micromamba --strip-components=1 bin/micromamba || rm -f /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2) && \
      rm -f /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      /opt/micromamba/micromamba shell init -s bash -p /opt/micromamba/env && \
      chmod -R 755 /opt/micromamba
  # Clone repository with submodules
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git && \
      cd Baleen-FAST24 && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Set up environment using pip instead of micromamba
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt && \
      pip install jupyter
  # Download trace files
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/data
  RUN chmod +x get-tectonic.sh && \
      ./get-tectonic.sh && \
      chmod +x clean.sh
  # Setup reproduce script and make executable
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/notebooks/reproduce
  RUN chmod +x reproduce_commands.sh
  # Create getting-started script
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen/Baleen-FAST24\n\
  ./BCacheSim/run_py.sh py -B -m BCacheSim.cachesim.simulate_ap --config runs/example/rejectx/config.json' > getting-started.sh && \
      chmod +x getting-started.sh
  # Set default command
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Set base directory
  ENV BASE_DIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      git \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.9 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-dev \
      build-essential \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install micromamba with verified URL and improved error handling
  RUN mkdir -p /opt/micromamba && \
      chmod 755 /opt/micromamba && \
      wget -qO /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 "https://micro.mamba.pm/api/micromamba/linux-64/latest" && \
      tar -xjf /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 -C /opt/micromamba --strip-components=1 bin/micromamba && \
      rm -f /tmp/micromamba.tar.bz2 && \
      /opt/micromamba/micromamba --help || echo "Micromamba verification failed"
  # Clone repository with submodules
  RUN git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/wonglkd/Baleen-FAST24.git && \
      cd Baleen-FAST24 && \
      git submodule update --init --recursive
  # Set up environment using pip
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN pip install -r BCacheSim/install/requirements.txt && \
      pip install jupyter
  # Download trace files
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/data
  RUN chmod +x get-tectonic.sh && \
      ./get-tectonic.sh && \
      chmod +x clean.sh
  # Setup reproduce script and make executable
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24/notebooks/reproduce
  RUN chmod +x reproduce_commands.sh
  # Create getting-started script
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  RUN echo '#!/bin/bash\n\
  cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Baleen/Baleen-FAST24\n\
  ./BCacheSim/run_py.sh py -B -m BCacheSim.cachesim.simulate_ap --config runs/example/rejectx/config.json' > getting-started.sh && \
      chmod +x getting-started.sh
  # Set default command
  WORKDIR $BASE_DIR/Baleen-FAST24
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
